<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Show tooltip on hover and focus</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Hide tooltip on Esc, click, pointer down, or scroll</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Only one tooltip shows at a time</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Labeling support for screen readers via <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-describedby</code></li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Custom show and hide delay support</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Matches native tooltip behavior with delay on hover of first tooltip and no
delay on subsequent tooltips</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the tooltip package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> tooltip</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tooltip&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The tooltip package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>To get tooltip working, you&#x27;ll need to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set up the tooltip portal (shared container for tooltips)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Add <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">triggerProps</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">tooltipProps</code> to the right elements</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:tooltip/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" </span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="customizing-the-timings" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing the timings<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-the-timings"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the tooltip opens after <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">400ms</code> and closes after <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">150ms</code>. You can
customize this by passing the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openDelay</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeDelay</code> context properties.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">openDelay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeDelay</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="changing-the-placement" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the placement<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-placement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tooltip uses <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://floating-ui.com/" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">floating-ui</a> for dynamic
positioning. You can change the placement of the tooltip by passing the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning.placement</code> context property to the machine.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">positioning</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">placement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;bottom-start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="adding-an-arrow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Adding an arrow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#adding-an-arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To render an arrow within the tooltip, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getArrowProps()</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getArrowTipProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getPositionerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getArrowProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getArrowTipProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getContentProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token comment">/* ... */</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="dismiss-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Dismiss behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#dismiss-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Tooltips close on Escape, click, pointer down, and scroll by default. Configure
these with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnClick</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnPointerDown</code>, and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnScroll</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnEscape</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnClick</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnPointerDown</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnScroll</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="making-the-tooltip-interactive" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Making the tooltip interactive<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#making-the-tooltip-interactive"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">interactive</code> context property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to make the tooltip
interactive.</p>
<p>When a tooltip is interactive, it remains open as the pointer moves from the
trigger into the content.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">interactive</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-open-state-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for open state changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-open-state-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tooltip is opened or closed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-tooltip" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled tooltip<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-tooltip"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> for controlled usage.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  open<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setOpen</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-open" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic open<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-open"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the connected API for imperative control.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setOpen</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the content */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the content */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="open-and-close-states" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and close states<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-close-states"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tooltip is open, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute is added to the trigger</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the trigger&#x27;s expanded state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the trigger&#x27;s expanded state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="styling-the-arrow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Styling the arrow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-the-arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using arrows within the menu, you can style it using css variables.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token unit">px</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-background</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">red</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tooltip machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ trigger: string; content: string; arrow: string; positioner: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the tooltip. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openDelay</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The open delay of the tooltip.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeDelay</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The close delay of the tooltip.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnPointerDown</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the tooltip on pointerdown.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the tooltip when the Escape key is pressed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnScroll</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tooltip should close on scroll</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnClick</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tooltip should close on click</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">interactive</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tooltip&#x27;s content is interactive.
In this mode, the tooltip will remain open when user hovers over the content.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the tooltip is opened.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-label</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">Custom label for the tooltip.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PositioningOptions</code><span class="d_block">The user provided options used to position the popover content</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tooltip is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the tooltip</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the tooltip when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the tooltip.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tooltip <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tooltip is open.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to open the tooltip.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">reposition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(options?: Partial&lt;PositioningOptions&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to reposition the popover</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Trigger</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>tooltip</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>trigger</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-expanded</kbd></div><span>Present when expanded</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Content</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>tooltip</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>content</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo get tooltip working, you'll need to:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSet up the tooltip portal (shared container for tooltips)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAdd \u003ccode\u003etriggerProps\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003etooltipProps\u003c/code\u003e to the right elements\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tooltip/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCustomizing the timings\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the tooltip opens after \u003ccode\u003e400ms\u003c/code\u003e and closes after \u003ccode\u003e150ms\u003c/code\u003e. You can\ncustomize this by passing the \u003ccode\u003eopenDelay\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ecloseDelay\u003c/code\u003e context properties.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  openDelay: 500,\n  closeDelay: 200,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eChanging the placement\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tooltip uses \u003ca href=\"https://floating-ui.com/\"\u003efloating-ui\u003c/a\u003e for dynamic\npositioning. You can change the placement of the tooltip by passing the\n\u003ccode\u003epositioning.placement\u003c/code\u003e context property to the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  positioning: {\n    placement: \"bottom-start\",\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAdding an arrow\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo render an arrow within the tooltip, use the \u003ccode\u003eapi.getArrowProps()\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003eapi.getArrowTipProps()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{6-8}\"\u003e//...\nconst api = tooltip.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n//...\nreturn (\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getPositionerProps()}\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getArrowProps()}\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getArrowTipProps()} /\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getContentProps()}\u003e{/* ... */}\u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n)\n//...\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDismiss behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTooltips close on Escape, click, pointer down, and scroll by default. },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled tooltip\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eopen\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e for when a user interacts\nwith an element. Tooltips are usually initiated when a button is focused or\nhovered.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Show tooltip on hover and focus\n- Hide tooltip on Esc, click, pointer down, or scroll\n- Only one tooltip shows at a time\n- Labeling support for screen readers via `aria-describedby`\n- Custom show and hide delay support\n- Matches native tooltip behavior with delay on hover of first tooltip and no\n  delay on subsequent tooltips\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the tooltip package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tooltip/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the tooltip anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the tooltip package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as tooltip from \"@zag-js/tooltip\"\n```\n\nThe tooltip package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nTo get tooltip working, you'll need to:\n\n- Set up the tooltip portal (shared container for tooltips)\n- Add `triggerProps` and `tooltipProps` to the right elements\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tooltip/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Customizing the timings\n\nBy default, the tooltip opens after `400ms` and closes after `150ms`. You can\ncustomize this by passing the `openDelay` and `closeDelay` context properties.\n\n```jsx {2-3}\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  openDelay: 500,\n  closeDelay: 200,\n})\n```\n\n### Changing the placement\n\nThe tooltip uses [floating-ui](https://floating-ui.com/) for dynamic\npositioning. You can change the placement of the tooltip by passing the\n`positioning.placement` context property to the machine.\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  positioning: {\n    placement: \"bottom-start\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Adding an arrow\n\nTo render an arrow within the tooltip, use the `api.getArrowProps()` and\n`api.getArrowTipProps()`.\n\n```jsx {6-8}\n//...\nconst api = tooltip.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n//...\nreturn (\n  \u003cdiv {...api.getPositionerProps()}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getArrowProps()}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv {...api.getArrowTipProps()} /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getContentProps()}\u003e{/* ... */}\u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n//...\n```\n\n### Dismiss behavior\n\nTooltips close on Escape, click, pointer down, and scroll by default. Configure\nthese with `closeOnEscape`, `closeOnClick`, `closeOnPointerDown`, and\n`closeOnScroll`.\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  closeOnEscape: false,\n  closeOnClick: false,\n  closeOnPointerDown: false,\n  closeOnScroll: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Making the tooltip interactive\n\nSet the `interactive` context property to `true` to make the tooltip\ninteractive.\n\nWhen a tooltip is interactive, it remains open as the pointer moves from the\ntrigger into the content.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  interactive: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for open state changes\n\nWhen the tooltip is opened or closed, the `onOpenChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    console.log(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled tooltip\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` for controlled usage.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic open\n\nUse the connected API for imperative control.\n\n```jsx\napi.setOpen(true)\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the content */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"] {\n  /* styles for the content */\n}\n```\n\n### Open and close states\n\nWhen the tooltip is open, the `data-state` attribute is added to the trigger\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the trigger's expanded state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the trigger's expanded state */\n}\n```\n\n### Styling the arrow\n\nWhen using arrows within the menu, you can style it using css variables.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  --arrow-size: 20px;\n  --arrow-background: red;\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe tooltip machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe tooltip `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"tooltip\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"tooltip\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Tooltip\",\"description\":\"Using the tooltip machine
